                <h3 class="shengci-header">ğŸ’¬ <span class="zh">ç”Ÿè¯</span> (ShÄ“ngcÃ­)</h3>

    <script>
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {

            // --- Speech Synthesis Setup ---
            const synth = window.speechSynthesis;
            let speechUtterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance();
            speechUtterance.lang = 'zh-CN'; // Mandarin Chinese
            speechUtterance.rate = 0.9;
            
            let zhVoices = [];
            let voice1 = null;
            let voice2 = null;

            function loadVoices() {
                // Táº£i danh sÃ¡ch giá»ng Ä‘á»c
                zhVoices = synth.getVoices().filter(voice => voice.lang.startsWith('zh-CN'));
                if (zhVoices.length > 0) {
                    // Chá»n giá»ng Ä‘áº§u tiÃªn
                    voice1 = zhVoices[0];
                    // Cá»‘ gáº¯ng tÃ¬m má»™t giá»ng khÃ¡c
                    voice2 = zhVoices.find(v => v.name !== voice1.name) || voice1; // Náº¿u khÃ´ng cÃ³ giá»ng thá»© 2, dÃ¹ng láº¡i giá»ng 1
                }
            }
            
            loadVoices(); // Táº£i láº§n Ä‘áº§u
            if (synth.onvoiceschanged !== undefined) {
                synth.onvoiceschanged = loadVoices; // Táº£i láº¡i náº¿u danh sÃ¡ch giá»ng thay Ä‘á»•i
            }

            // Fix for some browsers that cancel speech on mouseleave
            let speechStopTimer;

            // Function to speak text, ensures it only plays once per hover
            function speak(element, text, voice) {
                if (element.dataset.spoken === 'true') {
                    return; // Already spoken on this hover
                }
                if (synth.speaking) {
                    synth.cancel(); // Stop any previous speech
                }
                clearTimeout(speechStopTimer); // Cancel any pending stop
                
                speechUtterance.text = text;

                // --- GÃ¡n giá»ng Ä‘á»c ---
                if (voice && zhVoices.length > 0) {
                    speechUtterance.voice = voice;
                } else {
                    speechUtterance.voice = null; // DÃ¹ng giá»ng máº·c Ä‘á»‹nh
                }

                synth.speak(speechUtterance);
                element.dataset.spoken = 'true';
            }
            
            // Function to reset speech state
            function resetSpeech(element) {
                element.dataset.spoken = 'false';
                // YÃªu cáº§u: Dá»«ng Ä‘á»c ngay khi rá»i chuá»™t
                if (synth.speaking) {
                    synth.cancel(); // Dá»«ng ngay láº­p tá»©c
                }
                clearTimeout(speechStopTimer); // XÃ³a má»i bá»™ Ä‘áº¿m thá»i gian
            }

            // --- Accordion Logic ---
            document.querySelectorAll('.accordion-header').forEach(button => {
                button.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    const content = button.nextElementSibling;
                    button.classList.toggle('active');
                    content.classList.toggle('open');
                });
            });

            // --- Chat Bubble Logic ---
            document.querySelectorAll('.chat-bubble').forEach(bubble => {
                // 1. Hover to Speak
                bubble.addEventListener('mouseenter', () => {
                    // --- GÃ¡n giá»ng Ä‘á»c dá»±a trÃªn bong bÃ³ng trÃ¡i/pháº£i ---
                    let voiceToUse = null;
                    if (bubble.classList.contains('left')) {
                        voiceToUse = voice1; // Giá»ng 1 cho bÃªn trÃ¡i
                    } else if (bubble.classList.contains('right')) {
                        voiceToUse = voice2; // Giá»ng 2 cho bÃªn pháº£i
                    }
                    speak(bubble, bubble.dataset.zh, voiceToUse);
                });

                // 2. Mouse leave to reset
                bubble.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
                    resetSpeech(bubble);
                });

                // 3. Click to toggle translation
                bubble.addEventListener('click', () => {
                    bubble.classList.toggle('show-translation');
                });
            });

                { zh: 'èµ·æ¥', pinyin: 'qÇlÃ¡i', vi: '(bá»• ngá»¯)' },
                { zh: 'æ’', pinyin: 'chÄ', vi: 'cáº¯m vÃ o, chÃªm vÃ o' },
                { zh: 'æ‹”', pinyin: 'bÃ¡', vi: 'nhá»•, láº¥y, rÃºt' },
                { zh: 'å“­ç¬‘ä¸å¾—', pinyin: 'kÅ« xiÃ o bÃ¹ dÃ©', vi: 'dá»Ÿ khÃ³c dá»Ÿ cÆ°á»i' },
                { zh: 'é²è¿…', pinyin: 'LÇ” XÃ¹n', vi: 'Lá»— Táº¥n' },
                { zh: 'ã€Šè¯ã€‹', pinyin: 'YÃ o', vi: '"Thuá»‘c"' },
                { zh: 'ã€Šç¥ç¦ã€‹', pinyin: 'ZhÃ¹fÃº', vi: '"ChÃºc phÃºc"' }
            ];

            // --- Flashcard Logic ---
            // Function to create and populate flashcards for a given grid
            function populateFlashcards(vocabArray, gridSelector) {
                const grid = document.querySelector(gridSelector);
                if (!grid) return; // Safety check
                
                vocabArray.forEach(item => {
                    // Create flashcard elements
                    const card = document.createElement('div');
                    card.className = 'flashcard';
                    card.dataset.zh = item.zh; // Store Chinese text for audio

                    const inner = document.createElement('div');
                    inner.className = 'card-inner';

                    const front = document.createElement('div');
                    front.className = 'card-front zh';
                    front.textContent = item.zh;

                    const back = document.createElement('div');
                    back.className = 'card-back';
                    back.innerHTML = `
                        <div class="pinyin">${item.pinyin}</div>
                        <div class="vietnamese">${item.vi}</div>
                    `;

                    inner.appendChild(front);
                    inner.appendChild(back);
                    card.appendChild(inner);
                    grid.appendChild(card);

                    // 1. Hover to Speak (only on the front)
                    front.addEventListener('mouseenter', (e) => {
                        // We attach listener to front, but store state on parent card
                        // Sá»­ dá»¥ng giá»ng 1 cho flashcards
                        speak(card, card.dataset.zh, voice1);
                        e.stopPropagation(); // Prevent bubbling to card's mouseleave
                    });
                    
                    // 2. Mouse leave card to reset
                    card.addEventListener('mouseleave', () => {
                        resetSpeech(card);
                    });
                    
                    // 3. Click to flip (for mobile)
                    card.addEventListener('click', () => {
                        card.classList.toggle('flipped');
                    });
                });
            }
            // Populate all grids
            populateFlashcards(vocabulary1, '#flashcard-grid-1');
            populateFlashcards(vocabulary2, '#flashcard-grid-2');
            populateFlashcards(vocabulary3, '#flashcard-grid-3');
            populateFlashcards(vocabulary4, '#flashcard-grid-4');
            populateFlashcards(vocabulary5, '#flashcard-grid-5');
            populateFlashcards(vocabulary6, '#flashcard-grid-6');
            populateFlashcards(vocabulary7, '#flashcard-grid-7');
            populateFlashcards(vocabulary8, '#flashcard-grid-8');
            populateFlashcards(vocabulary9, '#flashcard-grid-9');

        });
    </script>

</body>
</html>
